1. ëª©ë¡ì˜ ì˜ë¬¸ ë‚´ìš©ì„ eng-tradepub ìœ¼ë¡œ ì €ì¥í•˜ê³ , ì´ë¥¼ ë²ˆì—­í•œ ë‚´ìš©ì„ kor-tradepub ìœ¼ë¡œ ì €ì¥í•œ ë‹¤ìŒ, ê·¸ ë‚´ì—­ ì•ì— ì¼ë ¨ë²ˆí˜¸ë¥¼ ë¶™ì´ëŠ” ìŠ¤í¬ë¦½íŠ¸ë¥¼ ì•„ë˜ì™€ ê°™ì´ ì‘ì„±í•œë‹¤.
`cat read-tradepub.sh`
```
#!/bin/bash

if [ "x$1" != "x" ]; then
	file1="$1"
else
	file1="kor-tradepub"
fi
echo "#-- ${file1}"

if [ "x$2" != "x" ]; then
	file2="$2"
else
	file2="eng-tradepub"
fi
echo "#-- ${file2}"

cn=10000
while read line
do
	cn=$((cn - 1))
	echo "$cn:k=== $line"
done < $file1

cn=10000
while read line
do
	cn=$((cn - 1))
	echo "$cn:e=== $line"
done < $file2
```

`cat tradepub-name-made.sh`
```
#!/bin/bash

read_n_echo () {
	k_e=$1
	read_file=$2
	cn=10000
	while read line
	do
		cn=$((cn - 1))
		spcline="${line}          "
		reqmmddyyyy=${spcline:0:10}
		if [[ "x$line" != "xShare This:" ]] && [[ "x$line" != "xì´ ê³µìœ :" ]] && [[
			"x$line" != "xOPEN NOW" ]] && [[ "x$line" != "xì§€ê¸ˆ ì—´ë‹¤" ]] && [[
			"x$line" != "xDZone" ]] && [[ "x$line" != "xDì¡´" ]] && [[
			$reqmmddyyyy != "Requested " ]]; then
			if [[ "$line" =~ "ì¼ì— ìš”ì²­ë¨" ]]; then
				#-- 2023ë…„ 8ì›” 31ì¼ì— ìš”ì²­ë¨
				yy=$(echo "$line" | awk -F "ë…„ " '{print $1}')
				mm=$(echo "$line" | awk -F "ë…„ " '{print $2}' | awk -F "ì›” " '{print $1}')
				dd=$(echo "$line" | awk -F "ì›” " '{print $2}' | awk -F "ì¼ì—" '{print $1}')
				y2=${yy:(-2)}
				m1="0${mm}" ; m2=${m1:(-2)}
				d1="0${dd}" ; d2=${d1:(-2)}
				echo "$cn:${k_e}=== ${y2}${m2}${d2}-"
			else
				if [ "${k_e}" == "e" ]; then
					if [ "x${line}" != "x" ]; then
						line2str=$(echo ${line} | sed 's/ /_/g' | sed 's/:/-/g' | sed 's/;/./g' | sed 's/,/./g' | sed 's/- /-/g' | sed 's/â€œ//g' | sed 's/â€//g' | sed 's/(/./g' | sed 's/)/./g' | sed 's/</./g' | sed 's/>/./g' | sed 's/\[/./g' | sed 's/\]/./g' | sed 's/\//./g' | sed 's/+/./g')
						echo "$cn:${k_e}=== $line2str"
					fi
				fi
				echo "$cn:${k_e}=== $line"
			fi
		fi
	done < $read_file
}

if [ "x$1" != "x" ]; then
	file1="$1"
else
	file1="kor-tradepub"
fi
echo "#-- ${file1}"

if [ "x$2" != "x" ]; then
	file2="$2"
else
	file2="eng-tradepub"
fi
echo "#-- ${file2}"

read_n_echo "k" $file1

read_n_echo "e" $file2
```
